<script type="7f1e9c35ea5b5f1382b964fe-text/javascript">
    window.followersIframe = null;
    function followersIframeOpen(url) {
      gapi.load("gapi.iframes", function() {
        if (gapi.iframes && gapi.iframes.getContext) {
          window.followersIframe = gapi.iframes.getContext().openChild({
            url: url,
            where: document.getElementById("followers-iframe-container"),
            messageHandlersFilter: gapi.iframes.CROSS_ORIGIN_IFRAMES_FILTER,
            messageHandlers: {
              '_ready': function(obj) {
                window.followersIframe.getIframeEl().height = obj.height;
              },
              'reset': function() {
                window.followersIframe.close();

<script type="7f1e9c35ea5b5f1382b964fe-text/javascript">
(function() {

  var STORAGE_KEY = "ads_loaded_once";
  var started = false;

  function loadAds() {
    if (started) return;
    started = true;

    // تحميل GPT
    var gpt = document.createElement("script");
    gpt.src = "https://securepubads.g.doubleclick.net/tag/js/gpt.js";
    gpt.async = true;
    document.head.appendChild(gpt);

    // تحميل AdSense
    var adsense = document.createElement("script");
    adsense.src = "https://pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js?client=ca-pub-6749871118373128";
    adsense.async = true;
    adsense.crossOrigin = "anonymous";
    document.head.appendChild(adsense);
  }

  function triggerLoad() {
    loadAds();
    localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, "yes");
    removeListeners();
  }

  function removeListeners() {
    window.removeEventListener("scroll", triggerLoad);
    window.removeEventListener("mousemove", triggerLoad);
    window.removeEventListener("touchstart", triggerLoad);
    window.removeEventListener("keydown", triggerLoad);
  }

  if (!localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY)) {

    window.addEventListener("scroll", triggerLoad, { passive: true });
    window.addEventListener("mousemove", triggerLoad, { passive: true });
    window.addEventListener("touchstart", triggerLoad, { passive: true });
    window.addEventListener("keydown", triggerLoad);

  } else {

    // في الزيارة الثانية نؤخر 300ms حتى لا يضغط LCP
    setTimeout(loadAds, 300);

  }

})();
</script>

//<![CDATA[
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded",function(){
  document.querySelectorAll("img:not(.adsbygoogle)").forEach(function(img){
    if(!img.hasAttribute("loading")){
      img.setAttribute("loading","lazy");
      img.setAttribute("decoding","async");
    }
  });
});
//]]>
</script>
<script type='text/javascript'>
//<![CDATA[

// تأخير السكربتات غير المهمة
function delayScripts(){
  var scripts=document.querySelectorAll("script[data-delay]");
  scripts.forEach(function(script){
    var s=document.createElement("script");
    s.src=script.getAttribute("data-src");
    document.body.appendChild(s);
  });
}

window.addEventListener("scroll",delayScripts,{once:true});
window.addEventListener("mousemove",delayScripts,{once:true});
window.addEventListener("touchstart",delayScripts,{once:true});

// Lazy Load للصور
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded",function(){
  var images=document.querySelectorAll("img[data-src]");
  if("IntersectionObserver"in window){
    var observer=new IntersectionObserver(function(entries){
      entries.forEach(function(entry){
        if(entry.isIntersecting){
          var img=entry.target;
          img.src=img.getAttribute("data-src");
          observer.unobserve(img);
        }
      });
    });
    images.forEach(function(img){
      observer.observe(img);
    });
  }
});

//]]>
</script>
